Mwatana is an independent Yemeni organization involved in defending human rights. 837,UCzObwEuc6zYVyDkhwwP_Vfg,Cold Podcast,"On a cold December day in 2009, the mystery that still captivates America began.

Susan Powell was a regular woman. She was a wife, a mother, a co-worker, and church-goer.

She was also a victim, but of just what crime, no one can say with certainty.

She disappeared on a cold December night nearly 10 years ago. Her body has never been found.

KSLтАЩs Dave Cawley has spent the last three years examining tens of thousands of documents and recordings relating to the case of Susan Powell. He's uncovered evidence that has never before been seen or heard publicly -- information that brings this haunting cold case into a whole new light, many times through the words of those involved.

It is a project born in the wake of the 2020 pandemic, utilizing the advantages of the digital world to create music asynchronously. The goal of the project is to create music based around the criminal lifestyle, capitalizing on the vast metaphoric richness and creative possibilities associated with antisocial behavior. The band seeks to creatively invest in a culture that celebrates individualism, DIY attitudes and freedom from authority. By virtue of the inherent dissociative construct of a digital audio landscape, the band translates the loss of self, fractured communities, heartless corporate influence and rampant capitalism into hard-edged riffing, head-spinning rhythms, acrid, reality-based lyrics delivered with relentless resolve into an unwilling social diaspora.

╪▒╪з╪и╪╖╪й ╪з┘Д┘Е╪н╪з┘Е┘К┘Ж ╪з┘Д╪│┘И╪▒┘К┘К┘Ж ╪з┘Д╪г╪н╪▒╪з╪▒

The Free Syrian Lawyers Association (FSLA) is a Syrian non-governmental organization whose main goal is to enhance human rights and rule of law in Syria.  It was officially announced in 2012 and registered in Turkey. The FSLA strives to strengthen the alternative institutions that came to exist during the Syrian uprising by providing them with the necessary legal and administrative expertise. The FSLA operates in nine provinces inside Syria and and has implemented several projects including  arbitration  centers and Legal Clinics  , building the capacity of local councils, and training media activists on the use of video as legal evidence.",42,298,92539,UUQzWg6OzMpHp_wQdr7ZHZUw,TR,en-GB,"['https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Knowledge', 'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Society', 'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Politics']",2017-08-01,23:16:46,"['Knowledge', 'Society', 'Politics']",No,en-GB,ar,ar

3112,UCtZMzk8D3P4OixYTwsfPeKA,Illinois Criminal Justice Information Authority,"Created in 1983, the Illinois Criminal Justice Information Authority is a state agency dedicated to improving the administration of criminal justice.

The Authority brings together key leaders from the justice system and the public to identify critical issues facing the criminal justice system in Illinois, and to propose and evaluate policies, programs, and legislation that address those issues. The agency also works to ensure the criminal justice system in Illinois is efficient and effective. The AuthorityтАЩs specific powers and duties are detailed in the Illinois Criminal Justice Information Act [20 ILCS 3930 et. seq.].

3526,UCCQ3MUSukrN4YSPupzluxhA,Crime Investigation,"""Crime Patrol Dial 100"" is a popular Indian television series that falls under the genre of crime reality shows. The show aims to create awareness about various criminal activities, their consequences, and the efforts made by law enforcement to solve and prevent such incidents. Launched as an extension of the original ""Crime Patrol"" series, ""Dial 100"" focuses on real-life crime incidents and dramatizes them to engage viewers while maintaining the essence of the actual events.

The format of the show involves the reenactment of true crime stories, with each episode presenting a different case. The narratives often highlight the investigative process, from the initial incident to the resolution by law enforcement. The show features host Anup Soni, who guides viewers through the details of the cases and provides insights into the criminal justice system.
